			/* decrypt helper function */
		function decryptCharcode(n,start,end,offset) {
			n = n + offset;
			if (offset > 0 && n > end) {
				n = start + (n - end - 1);
			} else if (offset < 0 && n < start) {
				n = end - (start - n - 1);
			}
			return String.fromCharCode(n);
		}
			/* decrypt string */
		function decryptString(enc,offset) {
			var dec = "";
			var len = enc.length;
			for(var i=0; i < len; i++) {
				var n = enc.charCodeAt(i);
				if (n >= 0x2B && n <= 0x3A) {
					dec += decryptCharcode(n,0x2B,0x3A,offset);	/* 0-9 . , - + / : */
				} else if (n >= 0x40 && n <= 0x5A) {
					dec += decryptCharcode(n,0x40,0x5A,offset);	/* A-Z @ */
				} else if (n >= 0x61 && n <= 0x7A) {
					dec += decryptCharcode(n,0x61,0x7A,offset);	/* a-z */
				} else {
					dec += enc.charAt(i);
				}
			}
			return dec;
		}
			/* decrypt spam-protected emails */
		function linkTo_UnCryptMailto(s) {
			location.href = decryptString(s,7);
		}

skin-mb-l skin-mt-l"><div class="col col-sm-6 "><div id="content-c1747668" class="frame frame-default frame-type-text frame-layout-0"><header><h3 class="bigger "> GreyEnergy finally exposed </h3></header><p>ESET researchers just <a href="https://www.welivesecurity.com/2018/10/17/greyenergy-updated-arsenal-dangerous-threat-actors/" title="welivesecurity" target="_blank">unmasked the shadowy cyber-espionage group</a> dubbed GreyEnergy. It’s the successor to the BlackEnergy APT group which went ‘underground‘ a few years ago after terrorizing Ukraine until 2015. It’s also closely related to TeleBots, responsible for NotPetya, perhaps the most damaging cyberattack experienced. </p><p>Our researchers have demonstrated beyond doubt that GreyEnergy’s malware toolkit both <strong>mirrors and improves on already-sophisticated techniques</strong> used in the devastating NotPetya attacks and Ukraine power grid outages. </p></div></div><div class="col col-sm-6 "><div id="content-c1747666" class="frame frame-default frame-type-text frame-layout-0"><blockquote><p>ESET’s exposure of GreyEnergy is important for a successful defense against this particular threat actor as well as for better understanding the tactics, tools and procedures of the most advanced APT groups.</p></blockquote><p class="align-right">Anton Cherepanov, ESET Senior Malware Researcher</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="content-1747754" class="section faded-opaque skin-default "><span class="rimg section-image hidden" data-remote=".section" data-viewport="all" data-bg-color="faded-gray-lighter" data-src=""></span><div class="container" ><div class="section-content"><div id="content-c1747606" class="frame frame-default frame-type-image data-viewport="" data-src="https://web-assets.eset.com/fileadmin/ESET/INT/Banners/Others/technology-a.jpg"></span><div class="container" ><div class="section-content"><div id="content-uefi-firmware" class="frame frame-default frame-type-text frame-layout-0 skin-mb-medium skin-padding-m"><header><h3 class="bigger align-center"> Organizations at risk </h3></header></div><div id="content-c1747268" class="csc-frame csc-frame-default"><div class="row flex skin-gutter-l skin-padding-m skin-mb-s"><div class="col col-sm-6 "><div id="content-c1747289" class="frame frame-default frame-type-text frame-layout-0"><p>The consequences for organizations of all sizes can be devastating. Compared to BlackEnergy, GreyEnergy is a more modern toolkit with an even <strong>greater focus on stealth</strong>. ESET researchers have demonstrated that GreyEnergy has the capacity to<strong> take full control of entire company networks.</strong></p><p>One basic stealth technique is to push only selected modules to selected targets, and only when needed. In addition, some GreyEnergy modules are partially encrypted and some remain fileless – running only in memory – with the intention of hindering analysis and detection.</p></div></div><div class="col col-sm-6 "><div id="content-c1747609" class="frame frame-default frame-type-text frame-layout-0"><p>To cover their tracks, typically, GreyEnergy’s operators securely wipe the malware components from the victims’ hard drives. </p><p>The modules described in ESET’s analysis were used for <strong>espionage and reconnaissance</strong> purposes and include: backdoor, file extraction, taking screenshots, keylogging, password and credential stealing.</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="content-1747296" class="section faded-opaque skin-default "><div class="container" ><div class="section-content"><div id="content-c1747291" class="frame frame-default frame-type-text frame-layout-0 skin-mb-medium skin-padding-m"><header><h3 class="bigger align-center"> How ESET protects you </h3></header><p class="align-center">The good news is ESET can fully protect your organization. Our multilayered technology<strong></strong>combining machine learning, human expertise and global threat intelligence, <strong>combats exactly this type of new, previously unseen threat</strong>. </p></div><div id="content-c1747743" class="csc-frame csc-frame-default"><div class="row flex hidden-to-md skin-mb-l"><div class="col col-sm-4 "><div id="content-c1747744" class="frame frame-default frame-type-text frame-layout-0"><header><h4 class="bold"> ESET Enterprise Inspector </h4></header><p> Is the most flexible and custom-fit EDR solution on the market. It enables granular visibility and identification of anomalous behavior and breaches, risk assessment, incident response, investigation and effective remediation.</p></div></div><div class="col col-sm-4 "><div id="content-c1747745" class="frame frame-default frame-type-text frame-layout-0"><header><h4 class="bold"> ESET Dynamic Threat Defense </h4></header><p>Is a cloud-based sandboxing solution. It evaluates behavior of all submitted samples with threat intelligence feeds, ESET’s multiple internal tools for static and dynamic analysis and reputation data to detect zero-day threats.</p></div></div><div class="col col-sm-4 "><div id="content-c1747746" class="frame frame-default frame-type-text frame-layout-0"><header><h4 class="bold"> ESET Mail Security </h4></header><p>ESET Mail Security award-winning solutions provide powerful server malware protection, spam filtering, anti-phishing and thorough email scanning against all email-borne threats. It is compatible with all major email platforms.</p></div></div></div></div><div id="content-c1747749" class="frame frame-default frame-type-esetbase_fce_cta frame-layout-0"><div class="align-center"><a href="/int/business/enterprise/" class="btn ">Stay safe with ESET</a></div></div><div id="content-c1748107" class="frame frame-default frame-type-html frame-layout-0"><script>

	window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
	function ESETtrackClick(name,events,evars){
		dataLayer.push({ 'event': 'navigation', 'eventCategory': 'navigation', 'eventAction': 'click', 'eventLabel': name });
		if (typeof(s) === 'object') {
			s.linkTrackVars='None';
			s.linkTrackEvents='None';
			
			if (typeof(evars)==='object') {
			  var s_evars = [];
			  for (var evar_key in evars) {
				s_evars.push(evar_key);
				s[evar_key] = evars[evar_key];
			  }
			  if (s_evars.length) {
				s.linkTrackVars = s_evars.join(',');
			  }
			}
			
			s.useBeacon=1;
			//console.log(s.eVar13 + ' ' + name); // return false;
			s.tl(true,'o',name,null,'navigate');
		}
		//else { console.log('s not found'); }
	}

	let ESETAnalytics = {};
	ESETAnalytics.current_url = document.location.href.split('?')[0];
	ESETAnalytics.mmCat = $('#content-nav-main-level-1 a.link.active').attr('data-uid');
	
	$("#content-navigation .csc-frame, #content-navigation .frame").each(function(e) { 
		$(this).click( function() { 
			let id=$(this).attr('id').replace(/^content-/,'');
			let name=ESETAnalytics.mmCat + '/' + id;
			//console.log("MMclicked: "+name); 
			ESETtrackClick("newmenu-"+name,'',{ 'eVar13': ESETAnalytics.current_url});	
		}); 
	});
